posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:The most hygienic hotel I have ever stayed in!

Very few reviews - either too bad, or so good that I feel bad not to make a review. Beijing Wangfu Peninsula Hotel belongs to the latter.

Before the journey began, a staff member called to ask about the requirements in detail. I asked for an extra bed for a child, and the hygiene must be clean. I have high requirements for hygiene. I tried to stay in a super five-star hotel in Zhucheng, Guangzhou, and was scared by the disgusting scene of the toilet... I was blacklisted.

When checking in, the front desk confirmed my request again, and I emphasized the hygiene again. I said there was no rush, and the hygiene must be done well.

I was really surprised after entering the room. There were no stains on the carpet as I remembered, and no dirt was found, such as hair, paper scraps, food residues, etc.

The toilet was brushed clean. There were no fingerprints on the door handles, etc. Etc.

This level of cleanliness seemed to cure my cleanliness.

Breakfast: semi-buffet + ordering. No matter how many times you order, it is included in the buffet. No extra money is charged. I like ordering, exquisite and delicious.

Shower room: good facilities, good equipment, the shower door is waterproof, the water inside will not leak outside. Two kinds of shower heads with different water pressures are very suitable for relaxation and for children to take a bath by themselves. It is also equipped with children's shampoo and bath products. Very thoughtful and careful.

Adults and children like this hotel very much. Next time I go to Beijing, I will book the Peninsula Palace.

msg:Compared with the Waldorf Astoria on the opposite side of the peninsula, I personally think that the best point is that all the room types of the peninsula are designed as suites, cloakroom + living room + room.
This time I stayed in a 74-square-meter duplex on the 14th floor. The first floor is the hall + toilet, and there is a relatively long staircase to the bedroom + cloakroom + toilet on the second floor. Children are more interested in stairs, with carpets and staircase lights.
The overall decoration style is calm, with intelligent panel dimming, curtains, TVs, etc. In addition to the two TVs upstairs and downstairs, there is also a TV in front of the bathtub, and there is a radio in the cloakroom where you can listen to the BBC.

The breakfast in many hotels has been downgraded in disguise. The breakfast in the peninsula is okay, the fruit is fresh, and the quality of the watermelon juice is very good. You can order it. There are also some other Chinese and Western options. Although there are not many surprises, in general, there are still things.
The water delivery in the room is SIRMA, and the bottle is pretty.

Let's talk about the SPA on the peninsula. During the stay, I did two 1-hour facials. The product I used was the mystery of BR stock solution, and the price of a single session was about 1,500 including tax. What is more satisfying is that the beautician uses a variety of products according to the skin condition, from cleansing, exfoliation, moisturizing, various essences, masks, eye creams, and face creams. I am familiar with the product, and the working environment is also the expected five-star standard. Personally, I think it has some effect.
The price of the hotel's minibar and food delivery is generally a little expensive, but it is located in Wangfujing, so it is very convenient to buy anything.

msg:If you don't let me out of Beijing, I will be staying in Beijing hotels.
Pretending to travel all the time is our way to sweeten life
My birthday is also the first day of the new year, and I stayed in Wangfu Peninsula.
After a 16-year remodel, it's an all-suite hotel
I ordered a leveling once in 2017. If the impression is correct, it should be two rooms changed into one after remodeling. The area is doubled, the bathroom area is gratifying, and the interior decoration is calm, not the minimalist style that newly opened hotels like in recent years. I booked a duplex suite this time, and I found that I quite like this decoration style, so that it does not violate the roof ridge seen from the window. The area marked in the room includes stairs, so the area is actually the same as the 60-square-meter flat floor. It's almost the same, but the upper and lower floors are relatively more private, with the bedroom and master bathroom upstairs, and a separate toilet downstairs. The intelligent control system is relatively complete, and the tablet at the head of the bed can handle it. Downstairs there is a dining table for two, a sofa, a work desk, and even a printer, providing space for business guests to handle basic work.
The biggest feeling this time is, God, is the service of the peninsula so good now?
Before check-in, there is a phone call to the hotel to explain that the birthday will be checked in, and I hope to help arrange it. The lady who answered the phone said, "We have a few quotations for special arrangements..." I didn't have any expectations after hearing this. I brought my children to check in, and I didn't need to buy myself a birthday surprise, right...
After check-in, Ludi from the Guest Relations Depar**ent took us into the room and introduced the hotel's public facilities, floor layout, etc. When we entered the room, we saw a birthday light sign on the stairs and a serious birthday cake on the dining table (not sliced cake or Small pastries, the kind that can be shared by 5-6 people), and hand-painted birthday cards, I really feel the intention. I am a person with a high surprise point, and I am very happy this time.
Because there are stairs in the room, the colleagues in the luggage depar**ent will help to put all the large and small luggage in the required position, so there is no need to worry about the problem of climbing the stairs with luggage.
What is needed in the room, the response speed is also relatively fast
The only underserved depar**ent is the breakfast side of the lobby bar. First, we went to the bathroom after we were seated, and when we returned to our seats, we asked for the room number again. Then, for breakfast, there were two a-la-carte dishes for the main course and no additional orders were allowed. Other snacks and side dishes were self-collected. I was about to leave, I said "there's one more point", so she came back with a blank face, and I thought to myself, "This is the familiar peninsula." In the end, there were two waiters discussing the time before ten o'clock. It's time to order food....
Finally, the gym is the gym layout of the old hotel. The equipment room is not big, but it is basically enough. There is also a small yoga room with a Pilates bed, which can be used by basic treasures. There is also a small swimming pool inside, which is clean. The front desk service is also very warm and friendly.
In short, I was very happy to stay in this Spring Festival. When I come back, the service of the catering depar**ent must not be improved, otherwise I will not know the peninsula completely.

The hotel condenses the sense of culture and history of old Beijing and the north, which is unmatched by other high-end business hotels.
